<div class="leftcol">Meeting</div>
<div class="rightcol">Apr 24, 2018 - SPECIAL WORKSHOP/GOAL SETTING MEETING OF THE MARYSVILLE CITY COUNCIL - AGENDA - MEETING HELD AT 723 D STREET AT 8:30 A.M.</div>
<div class="leftcol">Category</div>

<div class="leftcol">Subject</div>
<div class="rightcol" id="ai-name"><span class="agendanumber"> </span>4. Public Forum - Individuals wishing to address the City Council on matters not already on the agenda are invited to make oral comments of up to three minutes. When you are called by the Mayor, please go to the podium and give your name clearly for the audio recording. You are requested to address your comments to the Mayor and Council, and not to the audience. By state law, the Council is not permitted to undertake any action or discussion on any item not appearing on the posted agenda. If you would like a response from the Council, please fill out a Speaker’s Card and you will be contacted within the next few days.</div>
<div class="leftcol">Type</div>
<div class="rightcol">Discussion</div>
